across several modules:\\n\\n**NIO-Based Selector and Channel Management** (org.apache.kafka.common.network):\\nThe Selector class (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/Selector.java) implements a non-blocking, multi-connection network I/O abstraction using Java NIO SelectionKeys. It works with KafkaChannel, which manages individual client connections and handles TLS/SASL authentication through pluggable TransportLayer implementations. The ChannelBuilder interface and its implementations (PlaintextChannelBuilder, SaslChannelBuilder, SslChannelBuilder) provide factory methods for creating secure channels.\\n\\n**Send/Receive Buffer Management** (org.apache.kafka.common.network):\\nNetworkSend and NetworkReceive provide size-delimited protocol frame abstractions for transmitting requests and responses. ByteBufferSend offers direct ByteBuffer-based sending. The Send and Receive interfaces define the contract for network I/O primitives.\\n\\n**Transport Layer Abstraction** (org.apache.kafka.common.network):\\nTransportLayer is an interface with implementations PlaintextTransportLayer and SslTransportLayer that handle the low-level reading/writing of bytes over SocketChannels, managing encryption and authentication protocols.\\n\\n**Request Channel Handoff and Server-Side Network Management** (org.apache.kafka.network and org.apache.kafka.server.network):\\nWhile the core RequestChannel, Processor threads, and Acceptor thread are implemented in Scala (kafka.network.SocketServer and kafka.network.RequestChannel), they are supported by Java classes for metrics (RequestChannelMetrics, RequestMetrics), session management (Session.java), and configuration (SocketServerConfigs.java). The RequestConvertToJson utility provides JSON serialization for request/response logging.\\n\\n**Connection Management and Quotas** (org.apache.kafka.network, kafka.server):\\nConnectionQuotaEntity, ConnectionThrottledException, and TooManyConnectionsException handle connection rate limiting. ClientRequestQuotaManager, ReplicationQuotaManager, and QuotaFactory implement request quota enforcement. (org.apache.kafka.common.network):\\nThe Selector class (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/Selector.java) implements a non-blocking, multi-connection network I/O abstraction using Java NIO SelectionKeys. It works with KafkaChannel, which manages individual client connections and handles TLS/SASL authentication through pluggable TransportLayer implementations.
